Tweet
Share
Pin it
Hola Applicants!
To help you cope up with your preparation, we have collated the interview experiences of our current batch students. The interviews were mostly based on the profile and background of individual candidates. We hope this would be insightful and all the best!
Full name Rajat Gupta College IIT Kharagpur Specialization B.Tech + M.Tech (Dual) in Civil Engineering Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (12) Organization(Name) Oceanergy Designation Structural Engineer Work Experience Background Oil and Gas Interview Location city Mumbai Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 5 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions None Maths/Stats questions https://qr.ae/TWILlI GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) No Is the interview stressful? No Tips for Written Exam https://www.exambazaar.com/blogpost/pgdba-course-exam Tips to fill Application Form https://www.exambazaar.com/blogpost/pgdba-course-exam Personal Interview https://www.exambazaar.com/blogpost/pgdba-course-exam Any other interaction post-interview ‚Äì
Full name Anadi Vashist College Hindu College, University of Delhi Specialization M.Sc. Statistics Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (23) Organization(Name) EXL Services Private Limited Designation Senior Business Analyst Work Experience Background Analytics/Consulting Interview Location city Delhi Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 4 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions Statistics Maths/Stats questions 1)MLE of Uniform distribution. X~U(0, theta) and then X~U(-theta, theta) 2) Hypothesis testing: How to formulate hypothesis? Composite null and alternate hypothesis testing? 3) Method of Moments Estimation 4)Linear Regression: OLS estimation and how to obtain normal equations? GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) No Is the interview stressful? Yes Tips for Written Exam Revise Mathematics of 11th and 12th. Start with basics, Ncert and RD Sharma for concepts and formulae. Tips to fill Application Form Nothing too specific. Personal Interview Revise Graduation Courses relevant to the course. Any other interaction post-interview ‚Äì
Full name Shubham Sureka College BIT Mesra Specialization BE Information Technology Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (36) Organization(Name) Olympeo Infrastructure LLP, ZS Associates, Snapdeal Designation Assistant Manager, Decision Analytics Associate, Business Analyst 2 Work Experience Background Marketing/Advertising, Analytics/Consulting Interview Location city Delhi Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 4 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions Few questions were there about my project I did at Snapdeal. I had to explain them the project. There were questions on Joins in SQL (some random sample data and they asked me to get a result). I remember briefly the question. Q1: There were some tickets along with their timestamp (created time stamp). Against each row, there was a column highlighting if the ticket if closed or not. Also, another columns showcasing the time when the ticket was closed. I had to find the maximum time taken by a ticket to get closed. Same for minimum. Also, how many tickets are still not closed? All using joins.Solution: Just do a left join on the ticket id and Mark the condition as closing date greater then opening date. Then calculate the difference in the time stamps (Closing-Open). Then group by functionality can be used to get the results.The discussion on this went for around 10-15 minutesKnowledge about Left Join and Inner Join was sufficient. They also made me write sub nested sub queries. The level was not very difficult. Maths/Stats questions What is correlation? Draw some examples? Basic idea about regression? They made me draw some graphs of some functions. They were bit tricky, but doable. GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) Yes Is the interview stressful? Maybe Tips for Written Exam Cat series (IMS or CL for English, DI, LR and few Maths questions) Do prepare Maths NCERT Miscellaneous exercises. In case you feel difficulty in some topics, brush up on JEE notes. Tips to fill Application Form Focus on what your work experience is. This will help you keep the interview in control. Don‚Äôt put lot of different things. Your form should be crisp and clear. For freshers and people with non analytics background try to do at least one project or course. This certainly shows that you‚Äôre interested for the course. Try to connect business and Analytics together. You can always quote some examples from your work experience or studies. This will convince them that you understand how analytics can be integrated in various business fields and will get you a brownie point üòâ Personal Interview I read all the techniques through YouTube. I prepared my CV points pretty well and to some extent I was able to keep the discussion around that. Jb statistics be a good resource for few basics. Any other interaction post-interview ‚Äì
Full name Srijan Gupta College Pandit Deendayal Petroleum University, Gandhinagar Specialization B.Tech in Chemical Engineering Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (18) Organization(Name) Defence, L&T Limited Designation Sectional-in-charge Work Experience Background Manufacturing Interview Location city Delhi Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 5 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions What is analytics? How do you relate yourself to analytics? Why is analytics a buzz word these days? Maths/Stats questions I was asked to solved an integral with cubic expression in the denominator. It reduced to a fraction of linear and quadratic expressions upon partial fraction. I forgot the formula for the standard quadratic at that time, so showed the panelist the expression formed. GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) Yes Is the interview stressful? Yes Tips for Written Exam NCERT mathematics is a great source for fundamental mathematics, and that easily got me through 75% of the maths section. The remaining question needed an extensive deductibility of NCERT concepts. Some standard AIEEE (JEE Main) book might be helpful. Do cover calculus portion judiciously and diligently. Tips to fill Application Form We were asked to provide our extensive background, including why you want to join this course, and hobbies. To answer the first question, I related the course to my long term goal and it made the whole process a cakewalk. Hobbies is something that should be genuine and something that you really are passionate about. the panelists can easily sense when a person is cooking up, and then they can grill you down even further. Personal Interview TIME mock interviews were a great help. To supplement the analytics domain knowledge, linear algebra basic concepts, normal distribution fundamentals, engineering level project management or operation optimization topics like decision tree and transportation problems might come in handy. Any other interaction post-interview ‚Äì
Full name Immidisetty Anudeep College IIT Kharagpur Specialization Civil Engineering Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (12) Organization(Name) Wipro Ltd. Designation Project Engineer Work Experience Background Software/IT and ITES Interview Location city Bangalore Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 4 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions 1. Why do you want to do PGDBA? 2. Applications of analytics in business. 3. How can you use analytics to develop the business of an MSME type industry Maths/Stats questions 1. Give real-life examples for Poisson Distribution. What are mean and SD of Poisson Distribution. Ans. Accidents occurring on a road, Number of Calls arriving at a call centre. Mean = variance = Œª. 2. Where does Normal Distribution meet X-axis Ans. At infinity. He tried to confuse me here. 3. Properties of Normal Distribution Ans. Bell curve, uncorrelated implies independence, 2 parameter distribution defined by its mean and sd. Generally fits most practical situations. 4. Differentiability of abs(x) Ans. Differentiable everywhere except 0. 5. How do you say when a function is continuous. Ans. When left limit = right limit = f(x) for all x. 6. How do you say if a function is differentiable? Ans. When left derivative = right derivative. GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) No Is the interview stressful? No Tips for Written Exam Arun Sharma ‚Äì Reading Comprehension and Logical reasoning books Tips to fill Application Form Be true. Do not overstate as it may back fire. Write only those points to which you can answer, discard those which you are not sure of. Try to connect your goals to business analytics. Personal Interview 1. medium.com 2. Probability and Statistics by WW Hines and Montgomery Any other interaction post-interview Also, they asked some Civil Engineering related questions as I was a Civil Engineering Graduate.
Full name Karthikeya R College IIT Kharagpur Specialization B.Tech in Agricultural and Food Engineering Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (11) Organization(Name) PhonePe Designation Business Analyst Work Experience Background Analytics/Consulting Interview Location city Bangalore Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 4 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions Hypothesis Testing, p-value etc. Maths/Stats questions Asked to Prove Pythagoras theorem [Draw the perpendicular from the right vertex to hypotenuse and use Similar triangles theorem] GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) Yes Is the interview stressful? Maybe Tips for Written Exam I would recommend practicing from Previous year JEE Mains Questions (Arihant) [only intersection topics], any popular test series (to improve speed). Tips to fill Application Form Write what is relevant to the professional background. Most of my interview was stressed over what was written. Personal Interview Questions on Matrix Linear Transformations, Mathematical Induction, Applications of Analytics in Payments Industry followed by Why PGDBA, General Awareness Questions, etc. Any other interaction post-interview ‚Äì
Full name KOLLI PARASURAM College NIT Bhopal Specialization B.tech in Electronics and Communication Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (33) Organization(Name) Bharti Airtel Designation Assistant Manager Work Experience Background Telecommunication Interview Location city Delhi Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 5 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions Nothing related to above topics. The panel asked me about work i do in my company. Then they asked if i know coding. I said no. Then they asked what i know in technical. I said Mathematics. Then interviewer asked what in mathematics and gave examples like statistics, probability. I said i am ok with any of the topic. Then they asked if i am comfortable with random variables. I said Yes and from that point interview started. Maths/Stats questions Q1. Find probability mass function of discrete random variable at one point giving its value at all other points? Ans:- Sum of probabilities is 1. So subtracted the sum of probabilities of all other points from 1 to get required answer. This took a good amount of time for calculation and gave correct answer. Q2. Plot the probability mass function of above discrete random variable? Ans:- I drawn it correctly. Q3. Find the probability of a continuous discrete random variable to lie between 1 and 2 giving cumulative distribution function (cdf)? Ans:- If cfd=f(x) then integrate f(x)dx with between lower limit 1 and higher limit 2. I did not solve it completely i drawn the graph and shaded area and wrote the integration form. Interviewer seen the equation and said it correct and not needed to solve completely. Q4. Find expected value of expected value of discrete random variable in first question? Ans:- summation of xf(x) from x=-infinity to x=infinity where f(x) is pmf in terms of random variable x. I answered it correctly. Q5. Find the expected value for the continuous random variable in third question? Ans:- Integration of xf(x) from x=-infinity to x=infinity where f(x) is cdf I answered it correctly. Then he asked if i know about situations of two random variables. I said i can do but only to basic level. Interviewer said he will ask basic level questions only and asked. Q6. Joint pdf of two random variable X and Y is given and asked to find marginal cdf of y where 0<x<y<1. Ans:- Integrate the x from 0 to y for the joint pdf to get marginal cdf in term of y. I answered it correctly. Q7. Find the probability of the function now? Ans:- We have to integrate the maginal cdf in y for its limits 0 to 1 where we get answer as 1. I got confused about the lower limit of integration here weather 0 or x. I took a bit of time in thinking and expressed doubt put x but he said it wrong then changed to 0. Sir( interviewer) later gave reason for it. Q8. Draw the plot of the joint pdf region? Ans:- I drawn the region 0<x<y<1 and shaded region on XY axis correctly. Full name Anurag Malakar College IIEST Shibpur Specialization B.E in Mechancal Engineering Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (22) Organization(Name) Maruti Suzuki India Limited Designation Territorial Sales Manager Work Experience Background Marketing/Advertising Interview Location city Mumbai Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 5 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions As I didn‚Äôt have any Analytics Experience and my background was Mechanical Engineering, no technical questions pertaining to the field of analytics was asked. Maths/Stats questions What is the probability that the digits of a randomly selected three-digit number will be in ascending order from left to right (without repetitions)?
Answer: 0 can‚Äôt be a part of the number. So, there are 9 numbers to choose from. When you have selected three digits out of 9, there are 6 permutations possible, out of which only in 1 will the digits be in ascending order from left to right.
So, total number of desired 3-digit numbers = 9C3 Total number of 3-digit numbers = 9*10*10
Probability = (9C3)/900

If you have done any analytics project or you have analytics background then be more prepared and have thorough knowledge. Try to know the maths behind it. Atleast have the intuitive knowledge. Because, I observed that panelists were grilling those candidates more who had prior experience in analytics. Also, fill the interview form properly. Specially the SOP section. Any other interaction post-interview ‚Äì
Full name Bharath Bhambore College BMS College of Engineering Specialization Telecommunication Engineering Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (58) Organization(Name) Oracle India Designation Solutions Engineer Work Experience Background Software/IT and ITES Interview Location city Bangalore Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 4 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions Functional questions like what factors would you consider while selecting a location for a base station. What inference can you get with ISD call data records? Maths/Stats questions Question was somewhat on the lines of: Given a circle of some radius, how will you get an equation for a chord of the circle. I‚Äôm not very sure if this was how they formulated it. Ans. Form a right triangle. Apply Pythagoras theorem. Differentiate partially with respect to length of perpendicular. You get a partial differential equation which is solved using one of the standard forms. GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) Don‚Äôt remember Is the interview stressful? No Tips for Written Exam Previous question papers, NCERT class 12 Mathematics books Tips to fill Application Form Past work experience can play a major role Personal Interview Go through Engineering Mathematics concepts learned in engineering Any other interaction post-interview Why did you choose this course? Explain your work etc.

Full name Swadesh College IIT Bombay Specialization B.Tech in Chemical Engineering Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (23) Organization(Name) ICICI Prudential Life Insurance Designation Manager Work Experience Background Software/IT and ITES, BFSI/Finance Interview Location city Mumbai Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 4 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions ‚Äì Maths/Stats questions Most of the questions were from Linear Algebra. I was asked to define rank,bases ,eigen values, eigen vectors of matrix.They asked me to solve for eigen values and rank of a particular matrix. No Tips for Written Exam ‚Äì Tips to fill Application Form ‚Äì Personal Interview Introduction to probability and statistics for engineers and scientists Sheldon M Ross (Basic statistics, distribution functions and probability), Basic Linear Algebra (enough material on the web) Any other interaction post-interview Major part of my interview was based on my work-ex and projects done there. Since I did my bachelor‚Äôs in Chemical Engineering one of the panelist asked me few questions on Mass transfer as well.
Full name Manasvi G College Indian Institute of Space Science and Technology Specialization B. Tech in ECE (Avionics) Work Experience (in Months) Fresher Organization(Name) ‚Äì Designation ‚Äì Work Experience Background ‚Äì Interview Location city Bangalore Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 5 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions What is MNF transform? Why did I use MNF transform instead of a simple PCA during satellite image processing? Maths/Stats questions Since I was a fresher from the space science industry, the first interviewer asked me as to why I wanted to shift from space to business analytics. I replied saying that my interest has shifted towards business analytics when I took electives like deep learning and optimization for operations research. I also mentioned that at the same time, my ‚Äòinterest‚Äô and ‚Äògrades‚Äô in electronics subjects were gradually going down. They asked me to model an equation consisting of these two variables, and they also asked me to first answer as to which variable was independent and which was the dependent variable. Initially it took me some time to understand the question during that period I explained as to how these parameters depended on various other factors. Later when I understood their point of view, I answered that interest is an independent variable and grades are a dependent variable as the grades depend on my preparation, my attentiveness in class, etc. The first panelist seemed to be very happy with my response and handed over the baton to the second panelist, who asked me questions about my internship which was based on satellite data analysis. GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) The third panelist asked me questions related to my hobby and was upset to see that I had written just three sentences for the given three blanks. He mentioned that everyone has written very short replies to hobbies. I described all the sentences in detail and they asked me about the different kinds of books I read, followed by questions about my other hobby which was teaching the lesser privileged kids. They asked me questions as to what I taught and which grade of students I taught. That shifted to languages when I mentioned that I sometimes teach in the native mother tongue so as to drive my point home and make the students understand more clearly. My next question was what are the official languages of Andhra Pradesh and then I was asked about languages of Kashmir. I took a wild guess, and also told them it was a guess. Everybody just laughed and a few guesses turned to be right while a few of them were wrong. Is the interview stressful? No Tips for Written Exam Math is the most important section. I think 11th and 12th NCERT math would be the best place to start and brush up basics and later go on to practicing advanced math problems. Data interpretation and logical reasoning are pretty straight forward, and easy to solve. Going through last year question papers would be highly beneficial as a certain trend can be observed in the question paper pattern and one can prepare accordingly. Tips to fill Application Form This is very important, especially for freshers because all the questions in the interview are going to revolve around whatever has been written in the application form. Do not forget to mention any relevant projects since they will add an edge to your profile and the interviewers can ask questions related to those projects as freshers will not have any work experience. Also fill in the hobbies section carefully and thoroughly. Personal Interview I went through the interviews of previous years and made a list of topics to study and go through. But at the end of the day, I‚Äôve been asked questions only based on whatever I have filled in the interview application form. I think its best to be authentic and candid throughout the interview process. Also, one should have a certain clarity as to why they want to pursue this course and how it would be beneficial to them in their future. The panelists are looking for candidates who have a keen interest and passion for business analytics. If they get a feeling that you are genuinely interested and have done your homework in this field, then the chances of converting the interview is very high. Any other interaction post-interview Why business analytics and why not space industry? This has been asked by two panelists. They were probably just surprised, the second panelist realized that I already answered and then he just said congratulations and all the best.
Full name Chetan Mehatre College NMIT Bangalore Specialization B.E in Electronics and Communication Engineering Work Experience (in Months) Experienced (9) Organization(Name) Cognizant Designation Programmer Analyst Work Experience Background Software/IT and ITES Interview Location city Bangalore Rating interview experience (out of 5 being very good) 4 Relevant Technical/ Analytics/ML questions Difference between supervised and unsupervised learning Asked some questions on my graduation project Maths/Stats questions Explain Normal Distribution What is Kurtosis and Skewness? What is the integration of mod x? Write the formula and explain Bayes Theorem GK/Current Affairs asked (if any) No Is the interview stressful? No

Hello Applicants!
First of all Congratulations for getting shortlisted for the interview round of the PGDBA 2018-20. To help you out with the preparation, we have collated some of the interview experiences of the students from the current batch. The interviews were mostly based on the profile and background of individual candidates.
1. Name  :  Amit Borkar
Work Experience  : ¬† Software, IT & ITES, 40 months
Duration of interview(in minutes)  : 20
What questions were asked related to your work experience?
What was your startup about? Explain briefly.
Any other startups you worked in?
What was your role in startup?
What questions were asked related to your college academics and projects?
No questions were asked about acads and projects.
What questions were asked related to Mathematics/Statistics/Analytics?
How comfortable are you with Stats and Probability?
A basic question on conditional probability was asked.
What questions were asked related to your extra-curricular activities/hobbies?
No questions were asked about extra-curricular activities.
What questions were asked related to current affairs and general knowledge?
Name the companies of Elon Musk?
Questions about Warren Buffet.
Questions about Arab Springs.
What questions were asked regarding your motivation to join the course?
NA
Any other question asked?
NA
Any suggestion for the candidates?
Be well prepared. Try not to bluff, say I don‚Äôt know.! Stay positive during interview, it helps. All the best üôÇ
2. Name  : Vishakha Bansal
Work Experience  : ¬† Software, IT & ITES, 36 months
Duration of interview(in minutes)  : 15

What all projects I worked on in Oracle ?
Despite my good experience , I want to leave Oracle and join this course . Why ?
What questions were asked related to your college academics and projects?
Being good in mathematics , why didn‚Äôt I pursue further studies in that field ?
What questions were asked related to Mathematics/Statistics/Analytics?
Definite Integral Question
What questions were asked related to your extra-curricular activities/hobbies?
I mentioned my hobbies in the interview form , they asked if I took part in any of the competitions ¬†or involved in some activities .
What questions were asked related to current affairs and general knowledge?
How can we improve the role of women in politics ?
Why law and order situation is not good in Kerela despite being the highest in terms of literacy in the state ?
What questions were asked regarding your motivation to join the course?
What made me choose Data Analytics ?
What do I expect from this course ?
Any other question asked? ‚Äì No
Any suggestion for the candidates?
Keep the answers to the point.
3. Name  : Manoj Mana

What is bootstrapping?
Types of biases in sampling data?
What questions were asked related to your college academics and projects? ‚Äì None

Define periodic function
Difference between convergence and boundedness of a sequence
What questions were asked related to your extra-curricular activities/hobbies? ‚Äì None
What questions were asked related to current affairs and general knowledge?
Since I am from Telangana, my views on Telangana separate statehood
Do you support Aadhar system?
A data breach in the ¬†Aadhar system might be a national security concern, do you still support the system given this shortcoming
Which other country follows a Aadhar like system?
Do you support Edward Snowden? Why/Why not?
What questions were asked regarding your motivation to join the course?
What do you intend to learn from this course
Any other question asked? ‚Äì None
Any suggestion for the candidates?
If you are a fresher, expect more questions from math. If you have experience questions will mostly be related to your work. Be adept in current affairs.

6. Name :  Tajendra Mehta
Work Experience :  ¬† Consulting/Analytics, 21 months
Duration of interview(in minutes) :  20
What questions were asked related to your work experience?
I was asked about the nature of my work.
What level of exposure to analytics I had in the different projects.
What questions were asked related to your college academics and projects? ‚Äì¬† None
What questions were asked related to Mathematics/Statistics/Analytics?
I was asked two questions on mathematics. One on Linear Algebra and the other on calculus.
They asked me to define co-factor and rank of a matrix. I was given a system of equations and had to find number of solutions using rank of the matrix.
From calculus, I was asked to write the Leibniz integral rule (Interviewer didn‚Äôt mention the name, they said write the derivative of a definite integral).
What questions were asked related to your extra-curricular activities/hobbies?
I played squash in my college, so they asked me whether I still play squash or have I discontinued it.
What questions were asked related to current affairs and general knowledge?
Given that the Uttar Pradesh elections had recently concluded, they asked me about the possible reasons why Samajwadi Party lost.
Another question was whether Manmohan Singh right to join politics?
What questions were asked regarding your motivation to join the course?
What is your reason behind joining this course?
Do you think being good in Maths is sufficient for this course?
Any other question asked?
None
Any suggestion for the candidates?
They are judging your willingness and enthusiasm for this program. They look for your thought process instead of the right answer. If you are stuck in a problem, they will mostly guide you so that you can proceed.
7. Name :  Shubhank Bhandarkar
Work Experience :  ¬† Consulting/Analytics, 21 months
Duration of interview(in minutes) :  25
What questions were asked related to your work experience?
What is the domain you work on (at Fractal Analytics)?
Tell me about projects you work on?
This was followed by Analytics related questions
What questions were asked related to your college academics and projects?
None
What questions were asked related to Mathematics/Statistics/Analytics?
Mathematics:
You have 2 sets x & y. Both has values from 1 to 100. A pair is chosen with one value from x and one from y. What is the probability that both values are even?
Analytics:
What is Linear Regression? (Based on what i answered in question 1)
Directing towards a whiteboard, (which had some points plotted with line passing though points) What is this line called as? (Related to Linear Regression, it was the Least Square fitted line)
What are the methods to get the regression line? (MLE, ordinary LSE)
What questions were asked related to your extra-curricular activities/hobbies?
What are your hobbies? (Nothing more on that)
What questions were asked related to current affairs and general knowledge?
1-2 current affairs questions while wrapping up the interview
What questions were asked regarding your motivation to join the course?
None. (Maybe because of work-ex in Analytics)
Any other question asked?
None
Any suggestion for the candidates?
Be calm and take your time to respond to the questions. The interviewers are cool and give you time to think and even help in case you are stuck.
Don‚Äôt give up if you don‚Äôt know the ans. They don‚Äôt expect you to know everything. Just tell them your approach even if you think the ans may be wrong.
8. Name :  Yash Hansalia
Fresher
Duration of interview(in minutes) :  30 minutes
What questions were asked related to your work experience?
N/A
What questions were asked related to your college academics and projects?
N/A

What is a relation in mathematics?
Difference between continuity and differentiability.
Give a function that is continuous but not differentiable?
Explain what do you mean by hypothesis testing?
What is supervised learning?
Find domain of the following function:
sininverse(logx^3(base2))
Give a complex function that is continuous but not differentiable.
What are different type of distributions in statistics?
Explain central limit theorem.
What questions were asked related to your extra-curricular activities/hobbies?
Give details about your NGO experience?
What questions were asked related to current affairs and general knowledge?
Indian economy and poverty index
Unemployment
What questions were asked regarding your motivation to join the course?

What field in analytics?

Prepare basic statistics like different kind of distributions and their characteristics.
Prepare calculus of Std 11 and Std 12 NCERT well ( not complicated sums but just concepts should be clear)
Freshers will be grilled on academics.
Why analytics? question ¬†should be justified well.
9. Name :  Deepanshi Seth

The interviewers were very friendly and helpful. Be frank about your opinions and don‚Äôt try to manipulate things. You should be thorough with everything that you have mentioned on your interview form.

PGDBA 2016-18 Interview Experiences Part-2
Skip to content
Tweet
Share
Pin it
This is in continuation with our  previous blog post , adding some more interview experiences from the batch of 2016-18.
Adhikari Vushesh Babu ‚Äì Dual Degree ( B. Tech. + M. Tech.) in Information Technology, ABV IIITM Gwalior, 2016
Duration: 40 mins
HR question about the following scenario- Let‚Äôs assume many companies are willing to visit your college this year and you are made the placement representative for your batch. What Steps would you take so that you will get all the credit for your batch placements and not placement season? List some of your initiatives which you think will help you in taking that credit.
Having completed post graduation in Information Technology from IIIT, why do you want to pursue Career in Business analytics?
Questions in core engineering part- Merge sort or Quick sort and in what cases would they work better with examples, also explain their worst case complexities. Explain Dijkstra‚Äôs algorithm with an example.
Questions in probability and statistics part-If I were to toss an unbiased coin 10 times, how many heads should I expect? If the coin is biased and the¬†probability of head appearing is 1/3, then how many heads do I expect in 30 trials. Explain Taylor‚Äôs series and its uses. Where are complex numbers used in real life?
SUGGESTIONS ‚Äì Just brush up your knowledge on probability, Statistics and your engineering mathematics. Have a look at sorting and search algorithms. Also be prepared to answer why a¬†career in Analytics.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Shubhodeep Dey ‚Äì B.Tech, Chemical Engineering, NITK, Surathkal, 2013; 33 months of experience in Petrochemicals, Reliance Industries Limited
Duration: 20 mins
I had done a lot of projects during my job so they started with what is the most innovative thing you have done. As soon as I started with my answer, they started asking me random questions on the¬†assembly line (petrochemical industries don‚Äôt have anything related to assembly lines). I was able to answer some of them. Then they drew a curve on the sheet and asked me what is the covariance between the data points. I had a good idea about this concept so I could deliver. They moved on to probability and wanted me to visualise a binomial distribution for the number of defectives being produced by a lathe machine given a probability of finding a defective. I could satisfy them by writing down the equations. Some more probability questions followed on coin tosses. My interview ended with a concluding question ‚Äì what are the major oil producing economies which are not a part of OPEC?
All in all, it went fairly good, I got stuck on few of their questions but they were kind enough to guide me. You don‚Äôt have to know everything, what they are looking for is the approach to the problem. Confidence and clarity of thoughts are key factors. The written exam had a heavy contribution in the¬†final selection.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Parag Bhandarkar ‚Äì B. Tech. in Electronics Engineering, VJTI Mumbai, 2014; 23 months of experience as a Software engineer, Diebold
Duration: 20 mins
Describe your work experience. What are the¬†skill sets learnt during work experience? Domains worked on? Who are the competitors for my company (Diebold)? How will you use Analytics for ATM Industry? What is the reliability in Software domain? What factors affects it? Which affects more ‚Äì Software / Hardware? and why?
2 basic mathematics questions-Based on definite Integrals of some box function, Integration of some trigonometric function
SUGGESTIONS-I think admission committee looked for a balanced profile. It was also written on the¬†website that they will look for Academic, test score and interview performance. As my academic performance was very good, despite ‚Äúonly-good‚Äù performance in test and interview, overall weight got balanced.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Prem Krishn ‚Äì ¬†B.Tech. in Electrical Engineering, IIT BHU, 2011; 54 months of experience in Tata Steel (Manufacturing industry)
Duration: 25 mins
Based on my design experience in 3D modelling of Electricals at Tata Steel, they asked about my work in detail, then they gave the equation of a solid geometry and asked what does it represent exactly,
Based on a certification I had in Data Science and SAS from Jigsaw Academy,
What is p-value? (Some questions to test that I really know it), What is the lacking point in R? (I told about memory issues.)
They asked about my role model, some Current Affairs questions about him.
They seem to focus majorly on my prior knowledge about Analytics, genuine interest in the course and balanced answers.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Anshuman Roy ‚Äì B.Tech. in Electronics and Communications, Guru Nanak Dev Engineering College, 2011; 4 years of experience in TCS (IT industry)
Duration: 15 mins
Why do I want to go for analytics field after 4 years of work experience in IT? Which technologies and programming languages I worked on?
General formula of permutation and combination with their meaning and explanation with example.
Draw as many dots on a sheet of paper and asked how many triangles can be drawn in that many number of dots.
How many lines joining 2 dots can be drawn in that many number of dots.
Those days state elections preparations were going on in West Bengal. So I was asked 3 popular political parties of West Bengal, Delhi and Punjab, what are the major issues affecting people in these states, what was the issue going on among Kejriwal, Punjab and Haryana related to the¬†water supply to Delhi.
Questions related to programming as I had programming background. He wrote few numbers and asked me what will be the best algorithm to bring 6(a number which was in the middle of the series) to the second position. It was a question on sorting. They asked me to write down the algorithm.
SUGGESTIONS ‚Äì I guess they are judging your willingness and enthusiasm for this program. How much you can think to get to the answer. Sometimes they also look for your thought process instead of the right answer.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Swapnika Vajrapu ‚Äì B. Tech. in Chemical Engineering, IIT Kharagpur, 2014; 2 years of experience in Analytics in Banking sector, Crosslink Analytics
Duration: 25 mins
Questions based on my project at workplace which was related to predictive analytics like-
What were the dependent variables considered and what were the trends noticed? What was the mathematical equation used? Which tools were used? What algorithms were used? (Detailed description of the whole project)
Some basic questions related to machine learning algos which I told I was aware of. Mainly linear regression. What does the SAS output of linear regression model indicate? What‚Äôs the difference between causality and correlation?
1 basic question related to geometry- if you move 5 km¬†towards North, 5 km¬†towards South-West and so on, finally where would you be as compared to the starting point?
SUGGESTIONS ‚Äì They don‚Äôt expect the final answer to be correct always, they see the thought process involved in solving a problem. Be very confident about the projects you have mentioned, mainly which are related to analytics.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Shrey Manish ‚Äì B.Tech. in Mechanical Engineering, NIT Allahabad ,  2015; 1 year of experience in finance (trading), Futures First
Duration: 40-50 mins
Why PGDBA over other things?
On my work experience in the¬†trading industry, I was asked about the specifics of the products I traded, the different types of derivatives and how to take a buy/sell decision for an option class given a hypothetical scenario.
What are some probability distributions you know? Explain the Poisson and Normal distribution.
A couple of questions on linear algebra were asked which included solving a system of equations.
Discussion on the JNU row, wasn‚Äôt asked anything objective.
I was asked about the HR policies at my workplace and which of these were liked/disliked by the employees.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Sakshi Agarwal ‚Äì B.Tech + M.Tech. in Biochemical Engineering & Biotechnology, IIT Delhi, 2014; 2 years of work experience in Analytics (CPG sector), Fractal Analytics
Duration: 20 mins
The interview started with a brief introduction about myself.
Questions on work experience:
What projects did you work on?
Can you specify few important variables in the data you used in this project? How did you use these variables? What variables, you think, can affect sales of a company?
Questions on Statistics and Maths:
Do you know basic statistics?
What is hypothesis testing? Type-I, II errors? Test statistic? significance level? How do you define risk and decision making?
Given a signum function, discuss its limits and continuity, differentiability.
Some basic puzzle
In my opinion, they were mainly concerned about the confidence and clarity in the mathematical concepts and the reasoning ability of the candidate.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Mukul Sonker ‚Äì   B.Tech. In Electrical engineering, IIT(ISM) Dhanbad, 2016
Duration: 20-25 mins
There were 3 questions from statistics:
What is CDF? At a given point what will be the pdf? Can you derive standard deviation?
They asked most of the questions from maths after knowing my interest in mathematics. The questions are (not necessarily in order):
1. What is the differentiation of X!?
2. One question from definite integral.
3. Differentiate log X by first derivative method.
4. Integration of log X ( I was also questioned for a¬†particular method to find the solution).
5. Sketch the curve of log X+1 with steps.
Few questions on current affairs: Currencies of different countries . About maps. US elections?
They asked a few HR questions as well ‚Äì why we should not select you? Why I am not going for a job? My final year project.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Gunja Agarwal ‚Äì B. Tech. in Computer Science, Jaypee university, 2015
Duration: 35 mins
Tell me about yourself. Do you have other interview calls?
A puzzle was given to solve ‚Äì there are 3 bottles and a coin, so the probability of choosing a bottle is 1/3 but you have to get this probability by flipping a coin. What is the method to achieve the desired result?
Answer: flip the coin twice and assign each bottle a unique id i.e TT, HT, TH, HH. But there are only 3 bottles, so create a dummy bottle and assign HH to it. Whenever while flipping a coin HH comes, you need to flip it again till a bottle is chosen. This way we can form an infinite GP series.
Opinion on JNU event
Questions on Computer science subjects like- what is deadlock and some famous problem which is yet not solved? Name the layers of networking in order? What is a graph and difference between a graph and a tree? I was asked to write the pointer program in C and was also asked to explain it in detail
Feedback: In my case, I think my higher secondary school marks in mathematics and graduation marks help me to grab some brownie points. Also, I was able to crack the puzzle confidently that they asked in the beginning.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Kaustubh Daware ‚Äì B.Tech. in Electrical Engineering, COEP, 2015; 11 months of experience in FCA (Automobile industry)
Duration: 20 mins
I was asked about my work as testing and validation engineer in my company. They tried to relate statistics with my work.
Panel had given me a riddle and I was asked to calculate the¬†probability of the event specified in that riddle.
I was also asked to solve a problem on limits.
The interview panel asked me about my hobbies. When I told them that I like reading books, they questioned about my favourite books and what are they about. I was also asked that why am I pursuing PGDBA instead of masters in electrical as I had published few IEEE papers in my undergrad.
FEEDBACK: According to me, a fair idea on probability and calculus would suffice in cracking the interview.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Harsh Kumar ‚Äì B.Tech. in Chemical Engineering, IIT Delhi, 2016
Duration: 15 mins
What is linear regression?
What is the complexity of Dijkstra‚Äôs algorithm?
What is BFS (Breadth first Search) and its complexity?
Why do you want to be in this course?
One particular thing that you like the most and why?

Their major focus was on my knowledge of data structures and algorithms and some knowledge in economics.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Sidharth Kumar ‚Äì B.Tech. in Mechanical Engineering, NIT Patna, 2015; 2 months of work experience in Accenture (IT Industry)

What‚Äôs your position and responsibilities?

Any extra -curricular activities done?
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì
Ranjit Kumar Malloji ‚Äì B.Tech. in Computer Science, VNR VJIET Hyderabad ,  2015; 1 year of work experience in CA Technologies (IT industry)

As I was from Computer Science background, there were few questions related to the same. They asked me to choose a subject which I think I‚Äôm good at and I chose Database Management Systems. They asked me to explain different joins; how each one is different from the rest and asked me to write few queries ( 2, as far as I can remember). They also asked me to solve a problem on Bayes‚Äô theorem which we discussed for 10 minutes.

Few questions related to my hobbies, I told them that I am a gaming enthusiast to which they asked me what games I play.
‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äî‚Äì

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.

For written test, revise the topics taught in Engineering Maths.

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
Upon being asked which area of mathematics I was comfortable in, I replied linear algebra. The following questions were then asked-
Q1) What are eigenvalues and eigenvectors associated with a matrix? Some followup questions about the geometric interpretation of eigenvectors.
Q2) What is the cayle Hamilton theorem? Write the characteristic equation of a given matrix.
Q3) A fairly straightforward problem on finding the unconstrained minimisation of a cubic equation.
Q4) Question on plotting indifference curves of lexicographic preferences.
This was followed by a 7-8 minute long discussion on unemployment in India and what factors affect unemployment in a country, with special emphasis on the role of technology.
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.
The course and by implication the entrance process expects a fairly strong math background. Be thorough with the basics of linear algebra, unconstrained optimisation and probability theory. It will be of great help in the interview as well as in the course.

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
My interview went on for 12-15 minutes.
Panel: Tell us something about yourself
‚Äì I had a well prepared answer
Panel: Why you want to join PGDBA?
‚Äì Again I had a well prepared answer. I told them that I love solving maths.
Panel: So you love maths. Can you solve this question.
‚Äì They gave me a simple algebraic expression and asked me to explain it‚Äôs continuity and differentiability. I answered it orally.
Panel: Can you solve it on paper using fundamental equations.
‚Äì I did it.
Panel: Gave a question on limits.
‚Äì I did it.
Panel: If you have so much love for maths, why don‚Äôt you go for PhD.
‚Äì Told that PhD is more of theoretical mathematics and what I love is problem solving.
Panel: Have you appeared for any other management examinations?
‚Äì I answered.
Panel: What is your plan if you don‚Äôt get selected in PGDBA?
‚Äì I told them that I got placed in one of the IT firm and would pursue that.
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.
First of all be original in the interviews. I didn‚Äôt had any prior experience in analytics still I manage to convert the interview. All you need is the zeal to pursue this course and you should be able to convey this to the interviewers.

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
Three panellist one from each instituteP1- Tell me about yourself
Me:Told about my college , my current job as maths faculty at FIITJEE
P2: Ok since how long have you been working? Which all places have you worked?
Me: I worked at RBS for 5 and half months and post that I have been working at FIITJEE for the past 2 years.
P2: Gave a 2*2 matrix A and asked me to find A^n
Me: Answered it correctly. It followed a pattern in which after finding A^2,A^3 the result could be derived.
P2: Find e^A from the derived result.
Me: Used series expansion of e^A and obtained the result.
P3: Do you know programming?
Me: Yes sir, I did some C programming during my B.Tech.
P3: When did you pass your B.Tech?
Me: 2015
P3: x+y+z=10, find number of integral solutions?
Me: Infinite
P3: How about positive integral solution?
Me : 9C2
P3 : How?
Me: Derived using multinomial.
P3 : What if the values that x can take are [5,10]?
Me: Answered using multinomial using the given constraints on x.
P3 :interrupted fine you are doing it right. Do you only teach combinatorics or Probability too?
Me: +2 level probability sir.
P3: Given a single unbiased coin , how can you have equal probability of selection of 3 of us(referring to the panellists) in an exam?
Me : I was struggling.
P3: Ok if I toss two coins what will the events be? ( It was a clue√¢‚Ç¨¬¶)
Me: If we get
HH-P1 selected
HT-P2 selected
TH-P3 selected
TT-Coin must be tossed again
P2: How many times should we continue tossing again?
Me: Till we get a choice other than TT.
P3: Ok
P1: Any extra co-curricular activies you have done in state level or district level
Me: No sir
P3 and P2 : Ok best of luck for your results
Me: Thank you sir

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
There were three interviewers on the panel .I was asked to tell me something about myself and what I want to do next (probably an icebreaker). While I was doing that, they read my CV and asked me about my 3-month internship in Taiwan and the work that I did there. Following that up, they asked me about one other project in depth that I did in Physics. (They didn‚Äôt ask me about other projects that were mentioned in the CV which were in relevant fields, like Data structures and another one in Analytics). Then came the part around which majority of the interview revolved. The professor in the middle said ,so you are from IIT Delhi. I should assume you have amazing skills in Mathematics.I said you can say that. The professor sitting on the left asked me about double derivatives, maxima-minima, limits, continuity of 4-5 different functions, each time giving a more complex function and tried to test whether I knew what I was saying and asked me to draw a few functions. But the questions were quite basic and he seemed happy with the answers. *Over to the professor in the middle*. He asked me if my degree had a probability course. I told him that it didn‚Äôt but I did a course in Probability and Stochastic processes for extra credits in third year. He asked me to write the probability density function, the cumulative density function of exponential distribution and then draw both of them. When I did that, he asked me what a memoryless process is. I told him that the future state of the process depends on the current state of the process and not the past states . He said that is not the description of a memoryless process. I tried to make him understand in a few different ways but he said no. Then the professor wrote a differential equation that I had never seen in my life. He asked me what it was. I could only answer that it was a linear homogeneous differential equation because beyond that I had no idea. He said it is a linear homogeneous differential equation but what is the name of the equation. I looked at it and tried to remember but in vain. Then he said, it must have been taught to you in the first year. I said it wasn‚Äôt taught. He said, it is simply impossible. You need to go back home and look at your notes. I couldn‚Äôt argue as it would look bad on my part. *Already sinking in my chair* *Over to the professor on the right* He asked me that you have played basketball on a lot of levels as mentioned in your CV, tell me name of one player. I was relieved that he didn‚Äôt ask the size of the court or the ball which I had mugged up the previous night.I said Kobe Bryant. He asked who is the greatest player of all time. I said Michael Jordan. He asked me to name one player playing in NBA who is from India. I answered Satnam Singh. Then he asked me to name one player from team India to which I answered Amritpal Singh and the interview was then over.The written test had more weightage as inspite of not performing very well in interviews, I was selected.
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.
Ace the written test and for the interview focus on everything that‚Äôs in your CV very well

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
Q1. In a scale of 1-5 please rate the panel
Ans. I replied saying that due to lack of information I cannot answer the¬† question. I can give an answer after the end of the interview
Q2. Tell me something about yourself
Ans. Standard reply giving some introduction about my background, education and work experience
Q3. What is a KPI (on a point mentioned in my form)?
Ans. Key Performance Indicator. Then a brief discussion ensued for about 2-3 mins about how I got introduced to the term and how do I use the concept of KPI in my work.
Q4. How do you handle missing data?
Ans. I said that since my work revolved around working with Pharma industry data and we relied on certain predefined business rules to tackle such situations
Q5. A following question on any statistical techniques to apply in such situation?
Ans. I answered saying that due to preservation of information, we would like to impute such missing data. Gave them some basic techniques like mean/mode imputation. I said I am not aware about other advanced techniques
Q6. Question on my job profile.
Ans. I gave a brief introduction to my work as a Business Analyst and nature of my client‚Äôs industry. Some brief discussion of we used data to solve certain Business question.
Q7. if m,n are integers and m>=2 and n>=1. Solve the equation m^n=n^m where m is not equal n
Ans. I said that without loss of generality, n>=2 follows. A typical solution would be m=2,n=4. Then I was asked to solve the equation and tell the number of solutions. I started with a reasoning that such solutions would have m/n= a(some integer). Then we could plug it in the equation to solve.
Q8. A simple problem on how many handshakes would take place in a room of 100 people
Ans. 100C2
Q9. They gave me a integral equation to solve on a function f(x) and unknown constant
Ans. I replied that we can use Leibnitz theorem on differentiating integral equations. Then solved the equation and arrived at the value of the constant
Q10. Why would I go for this course and not MBA?
Ans. I found this question difficult in the sense that any cliched reply didn‚Äôt work out
Q11. If I walked along the border of the 7 sister states, what are the states that I would encounter sequentially
Ans. This question was asked as I had mentioned quizzing as one of my extra-curricular activities
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.
1. Be very sure about what you write about your work experience in the Interview application form
2. Have a very convincing answer to the question of choosing Analytics as a field of study
3. Have the concepts of maths till +2 level cleared well. Also for people having a work experience in Analytics, be aware of the mathematical foundation of any modelling techniques you implement in your job.

Me: 5th AASF Games, Jakarta Indonesia
TP: Okay Prem so tell me the agricultural situation in Maharashtra.
Me: (Told him various crops that are famous in various regions of Maharashtra)
TP: How can you apply data analytics in field of agriculture??
Me: I told him an Image application. He countered me with some problems to my solution. I told him solutions to them (atleast I tried to).
TP: Okay, Prem Thank You.
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.
PGDBA does not check only your technical prowess. It demands your ability to apply the knowledge for Business. And I would say Interview is very very important to demonstrate this ability. So prepare well for the interview if you get the call.

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
My interview started off with the standard tell me about yourself and my well rehearsed answer.With the unimpressive resume that I had, I couldn‚Äôt talk about my work experience or academic excellence. Instead, I spoke at length about my personality traits and aptitude that make me a natural fit for analytics and ended with my motivations for joining PGDBA.
Around this time, having gone through my file, one of the interviewers saw that my work experience had not remotely anything to do with analytics or data science and asked my how they tied together.
I admitted that they didn‚Äôt, that over the years, I had made some decisions and if I could go back and do it all over again, I would not make the same choices and that, I was looking for a second chance.
Then they asked me how good I was in Mathematics and if I remembered anything from the course ‚ÄòProbability and Random Processes‚Äô I had studied in UG. I said that I was above average and optimistically, good and no, I did not remember, but I had been revising some of the concepts. Then they asked me to solve the puzzle on the white board (It was a 4X4 grid where you had to calculate the number of paths from the lower left corner to the top upper corner). I had already come across that before and told them, and solved it on their insistence upon which I was given further cases on the same grid that I was able to solve.
Then, a brief discussion about why I shouldn‚Äôt pursue PhD instead of PGDBA ensued (I answered I would, after the course), concluding the interview. The interview time was about 8-10 minutes.
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.
Studying and practicing +1, +2 NECRT Mathematics books and solving the previous year question papers would suffice for the written test.
About the interviews, they just want to make sure that you are truly interested in the course. Just be honest and explain your motivations for the course.

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
Pre Interview process
My interview was scheduled on 1st April 2018. All documents were checked such as mark sheets and work experience certificate. There were 2 panels, each comprising of 3 faculty members belonging to each institute IIM Calcutta, IIT Kharagpur and ISI Kolkata.
I was 2nd last to be interviewed by panel.
Faculty 1 (IIT KGP): Tell me about yourself.
Answer: I answered as I had prepared.
Faculty 1 (IIT KGP): You have scored 9 pointer in fluid mechanics. Tell me about viscous effect in fluid. What is its formula? What is turbulent flow?
Answer: I could not answer this question. There was also follow up question on this but I could not answer it.
Faculty 1 (IIT KGP): What is Magnus effect?
Answer: I didn‚Äôt know but when he told it is about spinning of ball, I answered it correctly. It is based on pressure difference of Bernoulli Theorem. This is responsible for lift of Aeroplane wings and also used in Formula1 cars. This is also used in our vehicle bonnet and Aero Corner Design.
Faculty 2(ISI Kolkata): He asked a probability question like A and B are tossing dice repeatedly. A wins with 1/6 probability and B wins with 5/6 probability. A starts throwing dice. What is the probability winning of A.
Answer: It was easy answered it correctly.
Faculty 2(ISI Kolkata): It was linear algebra question using this formula (a+1)(b+1)(c+1)+1. Faculty asked What is sum of (a+b+c).
Answer: I did not answer it correctly. Faculty helped me with each step for correct answer.
Faculty 3(IIM Calcutta): He asked, Am I interested in current affairs?
Answer: Yes
Faculty 3(IIM Calcutta): There is some flood relief plan going by government, which are the states covered by them?
Answer: I answered Punjab, but he was asking more recent, U.P Government had also relieved farmers recently. Faculty then told me that It seems like you watch less news, which I agreed.
Faculty 1(IIT KGP): Asked me that they are finished. Do you want to ask anything?
Answer: I had to stretch a longer, so asked about How degree is awarded in these 3 institutes.
Faculties answered.
Faculty 1 (IIT KGP): Have you worked in TATA Technologies Analytics Division?
Answer: I said no.
Faculty 1 (IIT KGP): Is Girish Wagh Still at TATA Motors?
Answer: This was last question/chance so I elaborated How Girish Wagh is changing business, how he is leading business. Some of his recent initiatives.
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.
It does not matter whether you know analytics or coding at this stage, focus on maths topics and your core subjects.

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
Place of Interview: New Delhi
Panel of 3( each of them representing respective institutes), interview lasted around 20-25 minutes.Q1: Given to solve a definite integral question
Q2: Given a set of equations with modulus operator and asked to find minimum and maximum values of independent variable.
Q3: Asked to find optimal solution of¬† set of linear inequalities ‚Äì Solved using graph
Q4 : Asked to state pdf of poisson distribution and explain its application- I did read about basic statistics including probability distributions( khan academy videos are a good start for that)
Q5: Asked about Laplace transform- Couldn‚Äôt answer (didn‚Äôt prepare, I guess question was asked since I am from electrical background and concepts like Fourier series, Laplace, Z- Transform¬† are used extensively there, didn‚Äôt anticipate that questions regarding these can be asked too).
Q6: Asked about the work experience at LnT, and stuff related to my family business in which I was involved briefly.
Q7: Asked about controversy around Cambridge Analytica ( burning issue at the time of interview ) ‚Äì Answered with detailed information and also my personal views on the situation.
Q8: Asked about my hobbies, with related general awareness questions, and interview panel collectively trying to have fun with me. Answered most of them in the same spirit, ending the interview on a light note ( one of the interviewer asked a trick question about my hobby, I caught the obvious trick, and told politely that i know its a trick question, answered with a smile and left the room with the panel in splits.)Overall difficulty level experienced : Moderate.
PS- No question was asked related to any knowledge of programming packages like R and Python.
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.

Questions asked in PGDBA interview along with your answers.
First they asked me make the interview interesting: To this I started telling them about the automotive competition I took part in and then stated my interest about geopolitics for which they asked a couple of questions. I answered all them to the best of my ability.
Then I received some questions on calculus and Fourier series. I don‚Äôt quite remember the questions exactly but those questions were all of conceptual type and required a bit of algebraic manipulation.
Then I received certain questions on autonomous vehicles(I stated automobiles as my special interest) about the sensors and workings etc.
So as a whole the interview comprised of 80% questions on calculus and algebra and remaining 20 % on personal interest.
There were no questions on job experience.
Any suggestion for aspirants regarding preparation for written test and interview.
Keep your fundamentals clear on topics such as calculus, linear algebra, and plots of functions.All they are looking for is mathematical aptitude and awareness around the world.
Keep calm and stay focussed. Don‚Äôt let yourself get carried away with their facial expression. Be confident about whatever you say.
